	availableDates = [];
	for (var index = 0; index < availableIssues.length; index++) {

                $("#datepicker").datepicker({
                    showOn: 'button',

					beforeShowDay: enableAllTheseDays,
                    defaultDate: availableDates[0],

				function enableAllTheseDays(date) {
				var sdate = $.datepicker.formatDate('yy-mm-dd', date)
				//console.log(sdate);
				if ($.inArray(sdate, availableDates) != -1) {
				return [true];
				}
				return [false];
				}
				
function getissuebydate(artdate){  

	var htmlvalfontpage='';
	
    $.ajax({
        url: "https://www.enewspapr.com/OutSourcingData.php?operation=getIssuebyDate&epaperid=PUDHARI&date="+artdate+"&data=15", 
        dataType: 'json',
        data: { },  
       	success: function(result)
			{
				if(result.length>0)
				{
					$("#mydata").html("");
					$("#section-linetriangle-2").html("");
					
					for(var i=0;i<result.length;i++)
					{
						
						var date=result[i].date;
						var splitdate = date.split("-");
						var newdate = splitdate[2]+"-"+splitdate[1]+"-"+splitdate[0];
						var issueid=result[i].issueid;
					
						var editionname = result[i].edition_description;
						var edname = encodeURIComponent(editionname);
						var editionid = result[i].edition_id;
						var edidsplit = editionid.split("_");
						var imgname = result[i].imagename;
						var pathsplit = imgname.split("/");
						var pathnewsplit = pathsplit[6];
						var imgNamenew = pathnewsplit.split("_");
						//console.log(result[i].imagename); 
						//console.log("data");
						  
						    /* var n = 5;
                           var dateMnsFive = moment(Date.now()).subtract(n , 'day');
						   var dateMnsFiveq=moment(dateMnsFive).format('Y-MM-DD');
						   console.log(dateMnsFiveq);   
						   console.log(Date.now());      */  
							
							
							
							

						/* var nck = imgNamenew[1].length;
						if(nck = 1)
						{   
							var IMgName = '0'+imgNamenew[1];
						}
						else{
							var IMgName = imgNamenew[1];
						}
						var imgname = imgNamenew[0]+"_"+IMgName+"_"+imgNamenew[2]; */
						
						   
											if(artdate <= archivedate)  
	{
		var imgpath = "https://s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/erelegos3dec17/News/"+imgname;
		//var link = "archive/editionpage.php?edn="+edname+"&date="+newdate+"&edid="+editionid+"&pid="+editionid+"&pn=1";
		var link = "editionpage.php?edn="+edname+"&date="+newdate+"&edid="+editionid+"&pid="+editionid+"&issueid="+issueid+"&pn=1";
	}    
	else{
		var imgpath = "https://www.enewspapr.com//News/"+imgname;
		var link = "editionpage.php?edn="+edname+"&date="+newdate+"&edid="+editionid+"&pid="+editionid+"&issueid="+issueid+"&pn=1";
	}

						
						htmlvalfontpage=htmlvalfontpage + "<div class='col-md-4'><div class='img-section'><h3 class='ed-heading'><span>"+editionname+"</span></h3><a href="+link+" target='_blank'><div class='img' style='overflow:none'><img  src='"+imgpath+"' alt='' style='color:#fff;'></div></a><h3><span>"+date+"</span></h3></div></div>";
					}  
					
					$("#mydata").append(htmlvalfontpage);
				}
				else
				{
					alert("Sorry! No issues found");
				}
				
			},
			error: function(xhr){
				alert("An error occured: " + xhr.status + " " + xhr.statusText);
			}

    });
	var splitavdate = artdate.split("-");
					var Year = splitavdate[0];
					var month = splitavdate[1];
					var date = splitavdate[2];
					var newDate = new Date(Year + '/' + month + '/' + date);
			        var monthNames = [ "Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "July", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec" ]; 
			        var changedDate = monthNames[newDate.getMonth()] + ' '  + newDate.getDate() +  ' ' + newDate.getFullYear();
	$("#textdate").html("");
                $('#textdate').html(changedDate);

}

		});

	 <script>
var acc = document.getElementsByClassName("accordion");
var i;

for (i = 0; i < acc.length; i++) {
  acc[i].onclick = function() {
    this.classList.toggle("active");
    var panel = this.nextElementSibling;
    if (panel.style.maxHeight){
      panel.style.maxHeight = null;
    } else {
      panel.style.maxHeight = panel.scrollHeight + "px";
    } 
  }
}
